				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					6 Cello Suites, BWV 1007-1012 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div><table style="padding:0.5em; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; background-color:rgb(245,245,245); width:70%; border:1px solid #a3bfb1"><tr><td width="42px" valign="top"><a href="/wiki/File:Ambox_notice.png" class="image"><img alt="Ambox notice.png" src="/images/c/c8/Ambox_notice.png" width="40" height="40" /></a></td><td align="center">
This page is <b>only</b> for <b>complete</b> editions and <b>multiple selections</b> from the collection here. For arrangements, new editions, and the like see (or create) separate pages for individual works linked in the <b>General Information</b> section below.</td></tr></table></div>

</th>

<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>This edition without slurs was edited based on the manuscripts of Johann Peter Kellner and Anna Magdalena Bach. Normal notation version of 5th suite and transposed version (in G major) of 6th suite are included. <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://bachcellonotes.blogspot.fr/"><i>Editor's Notes</i></a></span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">6 Cello Suites
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="zh-hans, zh">无伴奏大提琴组曲</span>; <span title="zh-hant, zh-hk">無伴奏大提琴組曲</span>; <span title="eo">Suitoj por violonĉelo sola</span>; <span title="pl">Suity na wiolonczelę solo J. S. Bacha</span>; <span title="eu">Biolontxelo Solorako Suitak</span>; <span class="expandline" title="18 more..."><span title="ko">무반주 첼로 모음곡</span>; <span title="fr">Suites pour violoncelle seul</span>; <span title="ru">Сюиты для виолончели соло</span>; <span title="es">Suites para violonchelo solo</span>; <span title="en">Cello Suites</span>; <span title="ca">Suites per a violoncel sol</span>; <span title="fi">Sellosarjat</span>; <span title="hu">Csellószvitek</span>; <span title="it">Suites per violoncello solo</span>; <span title="de">Suiten für Violoncello solo</span>; <span title="cy">Chwe Chyfres ar gyfer Sielo Digyfeiliant</span>; <span title="nn">Cellosuitar av Bach</span>; <span title="ja">無伴奏チェロ組曲</span>; <span title="cs">Suity pro sólové violoncello</span>; <span title="hr">Šest suita za violončelo solo</span>; <span title="nl">Zes suites voor onbegeleide cello</span>; <span title="pt">Suítes para Violoncelo</span>; <span title="nb">Suiter for cello solo</span></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Aliases
</th>
<td><span title="ko">무반주 첼로 모음곡(바흐)</span>; <span title="ca">Suites per a violoncel sol de Bach</span>; <span title="it">Suite per violoncello solo</span>; <span title="it">Sei suites a violoncello solo senza basso</span>; <span title="it">Sei suites per violoncello solo</span>; <span class="expandline" title="4 more..."><span title="de">Bachsuiten</span>; <span title="de">Cellosuite</span>; <span title="nn">Seks Suitar for Cello</span>; <span title="cs">Suity pro violoncello</span></span>

<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 suites:
<ol><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Cello_Suite_No.1_in_G_major,_BWV_1007_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Cello Suite No.1 in G major, BWV 1007 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Cello Suite No.1 in G major, BWV 1007</a></i>
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Cello_Suite_No.2_in_D_minor,_BWV_1008_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Cello Suite No.2 in D minor, BWV 1008 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Cello Suite No.2 in D minor, BWV 1008</a></i>
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Cello_Suite_No.3_in_C_major,_BWV_1009_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Cello Suite No.3 in C major, BWV 1009 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Cello Suite No.3 in C major, BWV 1009</a></i>
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Cello_Suite_No.4_in_E-flat_major,_BWV_1010_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Cello Suite No.4 in E-flat major, BWV 1010 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Cello Suite No.4 in E-flat major, BWV 1010</a></i>
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Cello_Suite_No.5_in_C_minor,_BWV_1011_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Cello Suite No.5 in C minor, BWV 1011 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Cello Suite No.5 in C minor, BWV 1011</a></i>
</li><li> <i><a href="/wiki/Cello_Suite_No.6_in_D_major,_BWV_1012_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Cello Suite No.6 in D major, BWV 1012 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Cello Suite No.6 in D major, BWV 1012</a></i>
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
